    <div class="post post_single vc_row">
   
    
<div class="single_post_navigation"><a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/why-reading-is-so-important-for-children/" class="next_project">Next</a><a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/instilling-a-sense-of-purpose-in-our-students/" class="previous_project">Previous</a></div>
<a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/10.png" class="prettyPhoto "></a><div class="post-attachement"><a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/10.png" class="prettyPhoto "><img width="1200" height="565" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/10-1200x565.png" class="attachment-blog_tn size-blog_tn wp-post-image" alt=""></a></div><div class="sep_25"></div>  <div class="post_ctn clearfix"> 
    <!-- .title -->
    <div class="post-title">
      <h2><a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/5-ways-creative-math-instills-a-positive-math-mindset/" class="tiptip">
        5 Ways Creative Math Instills A Positive Math Mindset!        </a></h2>
    </div>
     <!-- .title END--> 
     <!-- post-info-top -->
         <div class="post-info"><span class="pi_cat"><a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/after-school-care/" rel="category tag">After School Care</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/positive-education/" rel="category tag">Positive Education</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/student-care/" rel="category tag">Student Care</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/student-care-center/" rel="category tag">Student Care Center</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/student-care-center-singapore/" rel="category tag">Student Care Center Singapore</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/student-care-centre/" rel="category tag">Student Care Centre</a>, <a href="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/category/student-care-centre-singapore/" rel="category tag">Student Care Centre Singapore</a>    <span class="pi_sep">|</span>    </span><span class="pi_date">12 November, 2022  </span></div>
    <!-- post-info END-->     
    <!-- .entry -->    
    <div class="entry">
      <p>Creative Math: Studies have found that a positive attitude toward math boosts the brain’s memory center and improves math performance.</p>
<p>Here we explore the 5 ways that PlayFACTO School’s Creative Math approach provides a positive attitude toward math.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>1.&nbsp;</strong><strong>We provide opportunities for success to boost confidence.</strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignnone  wp-image-14860" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/11-300x210.png" alt="" width="400" height="280" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/11-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/11-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/11.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px"></p>
<p>We start with simple problems and slowly move to the more complicated ones. Encouraging children to retry challenging problems that they have failed to solve after learning and understanding more. This way they achieve success and their confidence in math increases.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2>2. We encourage perseverance&nbsp;when solving math problems.</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone  wp-image-14861" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/12-300x210.png" alt="" width="400" height="280" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/12-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/12-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/12.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px"></p>
<p>Explain that it is ok to be confused by a problem and try many different ways to get to the solution. It is all part of learning. Practicing perseverance to work through the initial frustration of not knowing where to start is the first step to building problem-solving resilience in students.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>3.&nbsp;</strong><strong>We give constructive feedback.</strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignnone  wp-image-14862" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/13-300x210.png" alt="" width="400" height="280" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/13-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/13-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/13.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px"></p>
<p>Give children constructive and honest feedback without praise or judgment. For example “I’m noticing that you know how to solve one-digit by two-digit multiplication and you need more practice with two-digit by two-digit multiplication. Pay more attention to the place value.”</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>4.&nbsp;</strong><strong>We teach Problem-solving Strategies.</strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignnone  wp-image-14863" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/14-300x210.png" alt="" width="400" height="280" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/14-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/14-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/14.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px"></p>
<p>Encourage children to experiment with different approaches when solving problems. There is often more than one way to solve a math problem. Teach problem-solving strategies that will help them tackle different types of problems. Here are some ways we teach problem-solving strategies:</p>
<p>1. Creating a Diagram or Drawing a picture</p>
<p>2. Guessing and checking</p>
<p>3.&nbsp;Making a table or a list</p>
<p>4.&nbsp;Logical reasoning.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2><strong>5.&nbsp;</strong><strong>We make practice fun!</strong></h2>
<p><img class="alignnone  wp-image-14864" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/15-300x210.png" alt="" width="400" height="280" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/15-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/15-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/15.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px"></p>
<p>Practice drills are required for better understanding, fluency, and automation. However, repeated practice can often become boring and tiring. Give practice assignments in chunks and keep them short. Try out many different ways of practicing like worksheets, digital games, board/card games, and even physically active games.<strong>&nbsp;Provide manipulatives for better understanding.</strong>&nbsp;Design your own games with themes and toys that your child will enjoy, like toy cars, dolls, blocks, and more. You know your child better than anyone and you know what gets them excited. Make practice time a fun time. You can find many ideas online on how to use everyday objects and toys like legos to practice math.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Find out more about our 38 Collaborative Learning Centres Islandwide!</p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-14614" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-300x300.png" alt="" width="300" height="300" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-300x300.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-150x150.png 150w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-768x768.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-570x570.png 570w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px"></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">H/T: <a href="https://mathcurious.com/2020/03/06/how-to-foster-a-positive-attitude-towards-math-at-home/">Mathcurious</a></span></p>
<h6><span style="font-weight: 400;"><img class="wp-image-9652 size-medium alignleft" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1-300x94.png" alt="" width="300" height="94" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1-300x94.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1.png 480w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px"></span></h6>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
